\wd witch
\thes witch
\nt The English terms 'witch', 'witchcraft' are used in Ghana English
and some anthropological studies to refer to people who harm
others by non-material means, whether voluntarily or involuntarily,
according to a complex of beliefs which is similar in general but
different in detail in each ethnic group.
\sd TN_ II.B.6.a
\td 24/May/2011

\wd witchcraft
\thes witchcraft
\sd TN_ II.B.6.a
\nt The English terms 'witch', 'witchcraft' are used in Ghana English
and some anthropological studies to refer to people who harm
others by non-material means, whether voluntarily or involuntarily,
according to a complex of beliefs which is similar in general but
different in detail in each ethnic group.
\td 24/May/2011
